1a1(1): sgyu 'phrul thal ba'i rgyud chen po zhes bya ba bzhugs so//
1b1(1): sgyu 'phrul thal ba'i rgyud chen po zhes bya ba/ dpal kun tu bzang po la phyag 'tshal lo// dpal ldan thugs kyi dkyil 'khor mchog/ thabs chen thig le bde ba'i don// sku
1b2(1): 'phrul dra ba mngon rdzogs pa'i// ma lus 'dus pa'i 'khor lo'i tshogs// lha mos bzhad dang rol pa yis// gnyis med bde bas tshim pa yi// lhan cig skyes pa'i ngo bor
1b3(1): gsal// ma lus bde chen rang bzhin du// snang zhes thig le'i ngo bor ldog/ thun mong thun mong ma yin pa'i// brtags par rang gi rtog tsam nyid// thabs chen gsang ba'i ye shes
1b4(1): gsal// nyi zla 'dres pa'i gar thabs kyis// gsang ba'i 'khor la dbang bskur bas// nam mkha' gang ba'i skye bo rnams// ma lus thig ler gsal 'gyur zhing // rol pa'i
2a1(1): gsang ba'i nyams ldan pa'i// thabs dang bcas pa'i bdag nyid kyis// thabs dang mdzad pa'i dgongs pa dag/ dus bzhir mnyam pa'i tshul du bzhugs// de nas
2a2(1): gsang bdag sprul pa'i skus// 'dod lnga chags dang thabs sbyor bas// thabs kyis gsang ba'i don ston pa// ma lus dgongs pa'i don thob pas// thog mtha' med pa'i thabs la
2a3(1): gnas// 'khor las thabs kyis pha rol phyin// 'khor ba thabs kyis bder son pa// thal bas brgyan pa'i 'jig rten du// 'dod pa lnga la ma chags par// gdul dka' ma lus
2a4(1): kun 'dul te// gsang ba'i don la smin mdzad pa// de ni thal ba'i dbyangs zhes bya// dus mthar snyigs ma'i 'gro ba rnams// gang dang bral bas ma smin pa// gang dag de dang ldan
2b1(1): bzhin du// 'gro 'ong med pa'i thabs chen pos// 'khor ba gnyis med don sbyor ba// 'di ni thabs chen rol pa'i rgyud// zhus dang de la dgongs pa'i phyir// 'di ni gsang chen thal ba'i rgyud// de tshe gsang
2b2(1): bdag mnyam 'dus pas// 'khor gyi rig sngags rgyal po yis// 'khor lo'i bdag po gtso bo la// 'dod dang mnyes dang tshogs kyi mchog/ dgyes pa chen po'i rol pas mchod// gsang ba'i don gzigs zab
2b3(1): 'i dbyangs// 'dod chags rol pa'i stobs kyis zhus// e ma ho gar mkhan 'khor lo bde// rtag tu bde bas bde ba'i mchog/ bde stong rtog pa gnyis min zhing // gsang ba gsang chen gsang ba'i
2b4(1): mchog/ 'dus pa'i 'khor lo sbyong mdzad pa// mtha' dbus la stsogs dus med pas// lhan cig skyes pa'i ngo bor gnas// thabs chen sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud// thun mong thun mong ma yin pa'i// gleng gzhi mchog
2b5(1): ni ji ltar lags// rol pa'i gsang ba las byung ba'i// sems kyi khyad par ci lta bu// gsang ba'i thabs mchog las byung ba'i// lha dang rtogs pa'i khyad par ci// sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i sku gsung thugs// rang
2b6(1): bzhin thabs las rang snang ba'i// dkyil 'khor mchog ni ji ltar lags// phyi nang gzugs brnyan byang chub sems// rig pa'i thig le mngon snang ba// khyad par rim pa ji ltar lags// gsang ba gsang chen
3a1(1): mthar thug pa'i// rim pa gang lags khyed kyis gsungs// 'dul ba'i skye bo snod ldan la// gsang ba'i dam tshig ji ltar sbyin// thabs chen rol pa'i dbang mchog gang // rig pa mchog la gnas
3a2(1): sbyor ba'i// rig pa'i brtul zhugs ji ltar lags// 'jug pa'i khyad par ji ltar bde// thabs bral log pa'i gang zag rnams// nges pa'i thabs kyis ji ltar dgrol// sngags dang snying po ji lta bu// 'dod pa
3a3(1): can la rol spyad pas// 'gro ba chags can ji ltar dgrol// zhe sdang can gyi gang zag la// rig pa'i bag chags ji ltar bsdu// las kyi khyad par ji ltar lags// rdo rje dril bu mnyam sbyor bas// tshad dang
3a4(1): dgrol ba'i tshad ni gang // thabs dang bral ba'i rnal 'byor pas// gsang ba spyad pas ji ltar 'gyur// thabs mkhas rol pa'i rnal 'byor pa// spyad pas lhun gyis ji ltar grub// 'das dang ma 'ongs rnal 'byor
3a5(1): yid ches bstan pa gang la snang // thabs ldan theg pa'i che ba gang // 'dul ba'i gang zag rgyal sras la// thabs kyi theg pa ji ltar sbyin// 'di dag thabs chen gsang ba'i don// ma lus bsdus par zhus pa
3a6(1): ni// dus gsum the tshom sel ba ste// rgyud kyi phyi mo zab mo mchog/ 'dod chags brtul zhugs mchog chen po// 'dus pa kun gyi rjes su gsungs// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'chang // lha mo'i tshogs dang gnyis med
3b1(1): cing // rol pa'i gar dgu rtse dang bcas// ma lus bde bas tshim mdzad nas// 'khor lo rol pa'i tshogs dang bcas// thabs kyis rol pa'i bde chen gyis// lus kyi dkyil 'khor dbab mdzad cing // bzhin
3b2(1): 'gyur ngag chad re dogs med// rnal 'byor pho mo rdul snyed bcas// rtse gcig bde ba 'bar bar byed// bde chen thig le'i tshul nyid kyis// rdo rje'i tshig tu 'di gsungs pa// 'di zhes nye bar mtshon pa ni// e
3b3(1): sogs rnam bzhi'i dbyibs can gnas// skad ces gsal byed las ming can// baM dbyibs thig ler bcas ston pa'o// ma da ma nus sdom byed yid// las can rnam shes de dag la// thabs chen tshig bral
3b4(1): nyams ldan pas// gsal bar go bas bshad par 'dod pa sgra don dam nges pa'i rgyud// yA na theg chen 'di yin no// dus ni bsam gyis mi khyab dus// nA ma de ming zhes bya'o// gzhan yang khyad par bshad bya
3b5(1): pa// thabs dang shes rab mnyam pa yi// sna tshogs bde ba'i thig le yis// de bzhin nyid du gshegs pa yang // sna tshogs zhen las grol bar bshad// bye brag brgyad cu bcu gsum pa// ma lus bde chen ngo bo
3b6(1): yi// bcud 'dus thig le chen po nyid// snang dang stong pa la sogs pa// brjod bya ma lus rdzogs par snang // rtog tshogs sangs rgyas bzhi bcu lnga// snang bas phye phyir gnyis su med// shes rab b+ha ga gsang ba'i
4a1(1): gnas// de dkyil pad+ma'i rim gsum po// gnyis gsum brgyad kyi khyad par can// mtha' ma gnas dang yon tan gyis// mngon par mtho bas 'og min te// las dang bcud kyis mtha' bral
4a2(1): ba// ye shes bzhi la dpag mi rigs// dgos pa 'byung ldan rin po che// ye shes lnga yi 'khor lo bskor// sangs rgyas ngo bo snang bcud kyi// spyi bor shin tu 'khyil bar gnas// nyung dkar sor gyis spags pa
4a3(1): ni// sa ya bcu gsum bde bas brgyan// sna tshogs ro dang ldan pa yi// 'dod yon khyad par can gyis mdzes// bde ba chen pos kun khyab pa'i// gang yang bde byed phyi nang bral// 'bras bu'i chos rnams rdzogs
4a4(1): par ldan// byang chub mchog tu nyi zla 'bar// de nyid bzhugs gnas yin par bshad// bcud lnga ye shes kho na'i phyir// dwangs snyigs med par kun tu gsal// sgra dbyangs gsung gi gnas bzhi yi// dbye bas
4a5(1): gsum gsum ngos gnyis dang // bzhi bcu gnyis su gyur pa yin// sa ya bcu gsum las rdzogs par// skye 'gag med pa'i ngo bos yang // rten can ji bzhin rten de bzhin// nyi zla thabs dang shes rab kyi// ro/
4a6(1): gnyis mnyam pa dus gsum bzhugs// dwangs ma'i thig le chen po yi// bde ba'i dngos por ye shes snang // thabs dang shes rab mi phyed pa'i// thig le gsang ba'i ro ldan pa'i// mtshan nyid kun bcom bde
4b1(1): chen po// rang gi ngo bo ma grub pas// rang bzhin lhan cig skyes pa'i phyir// bcom ldan de bzhin gshegs shes bya// gzugs stsogs lhag pa'i thig le ni// las dang yon tan sngon ldan phyir// rig pa'i rgyal po
4b2(1): nyid du brjod// bcud lnga 'dus pa'i thig le ni// rgyu dang gnas kyi kha dog ldan// ro dang las kyang de bzhin te// rang gi mtshan nyid kun tu snang // gang phyir 'byung sogs rang bzhin nyid// chen po'i bdag nyid
4b3(1): ltar snang ba// mkha' stsogs snying la gang gnas pa// nyams dang sbyor ba'i khyad par gyis// zab mo dag gi stobs las snang // khyad par rim bzhin shes par bya// mkha' sogs nang gi 'byung la snang // ye shes
4b4(1): 'byung lnga las dag gis// bskyed phyir dbyings su brjod pa ste// btsun mo'i dngos por de 'dod do// 'byung lnga sbyor ba'i thabs mkhas pas// thig le snod kyi khyad par gyis// til gang lta bu mkha'
4b5(1): gang ba// dkyil 'khor tshogs chen brjod mi lang // gang phyir thig les byin brlabs pa'i// rig pa'i tshul bzhi bsam mi khyab// rig pa'i rnam shes bde chen nyid// rang gi nyams kyis gnas pa'o// gsang
4b6(1): ba'i thabs ldan yul bzhi dag/ gang sbyor bde skyed btsun mo ste// bde ba chen por rgyas btab pas// lha mo nyid du bstan pa yin// dmigs sogs rang gi thig le ni// thabs chen thig ler mnyam sbyor
5a1(1): bas// las dang ngo bo 'bras bu'i phyir// sems dpa' chen po nyid du brjod// nyes zad byed phyir rdo rje ste// ma lus mi phyed bde chen las// rang gi gnas kyis phye ba'o// gzugs sogs nang
5a2(1): phyir rab spangs te// rang gi rtsa bcud bcas pa ltar// zag med thabs kyi rang bzhin gyis// bde ba bskyed phyir btsun mo'o// dus ni rlung gi go phye ste// byams pa la sogs ye shes bzhi// de bde rim pas skye ba
5a3(1): yang // ting 'dzin dbang du nges par gsungs// thabs dang shes rab mi phyed pa// gsang bar mnyam sbyor thabs kyi phyir// gsang yul dbang po'i rnam shes reg/ lus kyi chos bzhi 'dus spyad pas// ma lus
5a4(1): 'joms phyir khro bo ste// mtshan nyid las kyis phye ba yin// gsang gsum thabs kyi spyod pa nyid// rtag sogs mtshan ma las bskyed phyir// btsun mo zhes su bstan pa ste// las kyi skabs kyis mi gnas
5a5(1): pa'o// gsang chen thabs kyi rol pa'i rgyu// ma lus thig ler rang 'char ba// skal ldan thams cad spyod yul te// rigs chad dman pa'i yul ma yin// sgyu 'phrul thal ba'i rgyud chen po las/ gsang ba'i gleng
5a6(1): gzhi bshad pa'i le'u ste dang po'o// // de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba// thabs dang shes rab rol pa yi// sems lnga'i khyad par snang ba ni// thal ba'i rgyud 'dir bshad par bya// thabs kyi rol par gang
5b1(1): bskur bas// shes rab chags par gyur pa nyid// de bzhin shes rab thabs bskul bas// rol pa'i bde bas zhen pa sel// gnyis med rol pa'i sems lnga yis// rdo rje 'chang ba nyid du 'gyur// gzhan yang
5b2(1): rgyas par bshad par bya// thabs dang shes rab dbyer med pa'i// thig le mi phyed rang bzhin gyi// rdo rje phung po'i yan lag ni// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas lnga ru gsal// skye mched khams sogs ngo bo
5b3(1): nyid// sems dpa' sems ma'i rang bzhin no// sa chu spyan dang mA ma kI// me rlung gos dkar sgrol ma ste// nam mkha' dbyings kyi dbang phyug ma// gsang yul dbang po rnam shes reg/ ma lus 'joms pas khro
5b4(1): bopo ste// rtag sogs mtshan nyid las skyes pa// yum ste las kyi mi gnas bshad// yid chos bzang po bzang mo mkha'// chags sogs yang dag nyon mongs drug/ 'dul phyir sprul pa zhes gsungs so// thabs
5b5(1): chen snang ba rab bskul bas// shes rab thabs la gang bskul ba// phyogs bcu dus bzhi ma lus pa'i// snang grag gnas pa'i chos rnams kun// dra ba shes rab zab mo'i dbyings// gang la gang gis mi mtshon
5b6(1): zhing // mi shes byis pa'i yul las 'das// thabs la mi gnas de bzhin nyid// khyad par thabs chen sgyu 'phrul 'dis// skal med ma sbyangs skye bo dang // byis pa'i log zhen dge slong dang // mtshan ma'i rnal
6a1(1): 'byor yul ma yin// thabs dang shes rab rol pa ni// dga' dang bgad dang chags pa dag/ blta dang 'khyud dang 'dzin dang mnye// 'brad dang steng dang zhal sbyor dang // brtse dang gzhi ba dang rtsang
6a2(1): dang 'cha'// chags pa'i gar thabs sna tshogs kyis// tha mal snang ba bde bar thim// dzaHbaM hUM hoH'i phyag rgya yis// bzung dang 'khyud dang bsdams bskyod pas// gsang ba'i 'byung lnga la brten pas// rim pa lnga
6a3(1): ldan sems kyi ro// rim par 'byung ste gzhan du min// bde ba'i thig le las byung ba'i// skad cig zhen pa las 'das pa// bde ba'i ro ni gang skye zhing // rtsa dang thig ler bcas pa dang // thig le'i bde ba
6a4(1): nyams su 'char// gang tshe zhen bral bdes gang bas// yul sems bde ba 'gags pa yis// lhan cig skyes pa kun ldang ba// 'gags shing ldang bar bshad pa yin// rten las 'byung la ma brten pa// bde dang
6a5(1): mi rtog gnyis med pa// gang dang gang du rtag gnas pa// gnas pas de ni gnas pa ste// dus yun tshad las ma nges shing // rang gi rlung dang 'tsho ba dang // sbyor ba thabs kyi yan lag gis// rnal 'byor pho mo
6a6(1): rnam par mdzes// thabs chen thabs las byung ba yi// rig pa'i nyams la dmigs pa ni// gang du zhen pa kun bral ba'i// bde chen rang bzhin bsam mi khyab// 'di ni yul dang dbang po dang // rnam shes
6b1(1): dmigs pa'i yul las 'das// thabs dang shes rab 'dres pa las// rang rig bde bar rang gsal bas// ma lus thabs chen rgyal po nyid// rlung sems rten gyi thig le la// phyi nang dwangs snyigs rgyu ba
6b2(1): dag/ 'gro 'od med par gsal ba na// re dogs 'gro 'ong las grol ba// mthar phyin ye shes sems nyid ni// bde chen mi dmigs bsam yul 'das// bde ba'i thig le bcu drug pa// nyi zla 'dres pa'i
6b3(1): gar thabs las// phyi nang yul sems bcas pa dag/ ma skyes mnyam la gnas 'gyur zhing // thig le zung 'jug bde ba las// gsang ba'i nyams ni 'byung bar 'gyur// rten 'brel bde ba'i zung 'jug
6b4(1): las// mkha' ltar rang byung ye shes skyes// bde chen thig le rgyu rkyen 'das// rang byung ye shes gnas med las// sgyu ma'i cho 'phrul rang bzhin 'char// sgyu 'phrul dra ba bde chen po// rang byung rang rig yul las
6b5(1): 'das// skye 'gag gnas dmigs las 'das shing // 'gro 'ong bya byed las 'das pas// rang byung ye shes de bzhin nyid// sems kyi mtshan nyid gzhi rtsa 'das// mtshon pa'i yul la mi gnas pa'o// sgra
6b6(1): 'phrul thal ba'i rgyud chen po las/ sems lnga bstan pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// // de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba// thabs dang shes rab gnyis med pa// thig le nyi zla 'dres pa las// 'byung ba'i lta ba
7a1(1): bshad par bya// rdo rje dbang gi stobs ldan zhing // sngar byas thabs kyi bcud ldan pa'i// thabs ldan rnal 'byor nges pa yis// tsakra bzhi dang ka ba gsum// thabs ldan me rlung sbyor ba ni// man
7a2(1): ngag stobs kyis shes par bya// thabs ldan thig le 'byor pa yis// ye shes nam mkha' lta bur mthong // bskyed pa rlung gi phyag rgya yis// phyi nang drangs snyigs 'dres pa'i rlung // bzung dang mi bzung sbyor ba
7a3(1): yis// gsang ba'i thabs kyi rol pa las// ma skyes mnyam pa'i ngo bor mthong // steng 'og thabs la brten pa yi// zhu bas gnas thim bde ba'i ros// ma lus rgyas btab mnyam sbyor ba// bde chen thig le
7a4(1): stobs la gyur// gang de thabs las byung ba ni// nyi zla gnas bcud rang 'bar bas// gnas bcud thig le mi dmigs pas// spyi dang rang gi mtshan nyid gsal// gang du thabs chen las byung ba'i// steng 'og/
7a5(1): rlung gi sbyor ba ni// thabs lam bde ba'i gnyer dag gis// brtags pa rang gis rtog pa bzlog/ dngos po rnams kyi ngo bo la// bzlog bya nges kyang mi dmigs so// phung sogs rtog pa'i 'jig rten kun// log
7a6(1): rtog sgyu ma snang tsam las// nyi zla bden gnyis la nyid kyis// ma skyes mnyam la gnas 'gyur zhing // phung sogs lha yi dkyil 'khor du// rang snang rang gi mngon sum gsal// phyi nang nyams la brten pa
7b1(1): yi// kun rdzob thabs la mnyam sbyor bas// rang byung thig le rtogs byed cing // skye med bde chen klung du 'jug/ ma skyes bde ba'i thig le nyid// ma skyes pa dang bde chen dang // gnyis med 'dres pa'i thig
7b2(1): le nyid// yi ge gsum gyi brdas mtshon nas// byin rlabs thabs kyi sbyor ba yang // bde chen rang rig mngon sum gsal// thabs dang shes rab thig le ni// ma 'dres gcig dang du ma bral// thabs kyi bde
7b3(1): chen gsal gyur cing // bde chen gsal zhing mi rtog pas// zug kyang // seng 'khrug byin rlabs mi g.yo bas// ma lus dam pas byin rlobs mthong // thabs la goms pa'i man ngag gis// dngos po bde bar
7b4(1): nyams myong bas// rang rig phyi dang nang med nang // mi dmigs brjod med gang bsgom pa// 'du shes klung du zhugs gyur na// brjod pa med pa de nyid mthong // nyi ma zla ba rkyen phrad las// drod dang rlan
7b5(1): la thogs med cing // rnal 'byor thabs kyi rim bskul na// bde chen ye shes thogs pa med// gnas bzhi bcud ldan rang bzhin la// rkyen dang dmigs pa la brten pas// sems lngas thig le sngon sbyangs
7b6(1): te// ye shes nam mkha'i gzugs su skye// rtsa dang rnam shes rgyu ba las// thabs kyi gsal byed de goms nas// 'byung lnga bcud lnga phung por bcas// mi zad rgyan gyi 'khor lor mthong // tsit+ta snying po kha sbyor
8a1(1): dbus// chos nyid ye shes g.yas g.yon la// dbu ma dbyer med thabs bzung bas// sems lngas thig le mngon sbyangs te// phung po 'byung ba rnam shes bcud// grangs las 'das pa'i ye shes
8a2(1): kyang // mnyam pa lnga ru gsal bar mthong // rang byung mi shigs thig le ni// drangs ma ye shes lnga ldan la// sgron ma'i thabs kyis gang bskul ba// dngas ma bde ba'i rtags 'byung zhing // ma bslad ye shes
8a3(1): 'char bar 'gyur// phyi rol rgyu ba rlung bcad cing // drangs ma rim par zhugs pa na// rtsa bzhir snying po thim pa las// dngos po phyi nang yul 'gags pas// bde chen sgyu ma las byung zhing // ma skyes ye shes
8a4(1): gsal bar mthong // drangs ma'i nyams kyi rtags 'byung ba// 'dzag dang 'dar dang 'phar ba dang // rgyug dang glu dang sgra sgrog dang // 'bar dang bde ba 'byung ba dang // thar dang 'ching med mngon shes dang // skye
8a5(1): mched nam mkha'i rang bzhin gsal// thabs dang shes rab mngon sbyar ba'i// nyi zla 'dres pa'i gar thabs kyis// thig le 'khor lo bskur ba'i tshe// thabs ldan gnyis med bsal bar 'gyur// thabs
8a6(1): chen thabs la gnas pa yis// pad+ma rdo rje sbyor ba yi// gsang ba'i thig le zung 'jug pas// drangs te ma lus gang ba yis// phung po rnam shes lnga ru gsal// thig le thabs kyis zin pa la// lhan cig skyes par
8b1(1): rang snang bas// rtog pa'i bye brag rang 'gags shing // las dang skyon bral pad+ma can// bde ba'i thig le ma skyes pas// ma rig gnyis 'dzin la sogs pa'i// phyi nang bde ba chen po gsal// bde chen sgyu mar
8b2(1): rang snang bas// phyi nang bdag gzhan log pa'i sems// bde chen rang byung thig ler gnas// rang byung rten gyi thig le la// man ngag thabs kyi bde rgyas pas// dman pa'i mtshan ma ring spangs nas// rang byung
8b3(1): ye shes mngon du gsal// 'di ni 'jigs bral tshad ma ste// ngo bo nyid kyi bden mthong zhing // rang byung ye shes mngon sum pas// dman pa'i tshad ma rnam par 'jig/ 'khor ba mun pa'i phung po la// thabs
8b4(1): chen snang bas gsal byas nas// rang byung bde ba thog mtha' med// da lta nyid du gsal bar byed// thig le zung 'jug bde ba ni// sems mtha' ldog pas go phye nas// dkyil 'khor drug gi yul rnams
8b5(1): su// sprul pa'i thig le rang shar ba'i// snang ba'i mdzad pa bsam mi khyab// chags sogs nyon mongs la rtog ril// gdul phyir sprul pa zhes su bshad// sgra dbyangs gsung gi bstan pa rnams// nges par
8b6(1): grags pa kho na nyid// phung sogs rtog pa'i 'jig rten kun// log rtog sgyu ma snang tsam las// nyi zla bden gnyis la nyid kyis// ma skyes mnyam la gnas 'gyur zhing // phung sogs lha yi dkyil 'khor du// rang
9a1(1): snang rang rig mngon sum gsal// dus gsum du'ang mi 'gyur phyir// theg 'dir zabs dang snying rjer bshad// gang phyir 'jig rten mtha' yas par// mos pa bsam yas phyir gsungs
9a2(1): pa// bstan pa mtha' yas bstan pa ni// 'gro ba'i bsam pa ji bzhin no// gang phyir theg chen gsang ba'i don// thal ba'i rgyud chen bstan pa 'di// 'gro ba chags chen 'dul ba'i phyir// dug gis dug nad
9a3(1): bsal ba ltar// sgyu 'phrul chen po 'di dag yin// skyes bu thabs kyis bder 'jug pa// gang gis 'di dag bder sel ba// ma rmongs thabs la mkhas pa yis// pad+ma la ni 'dam bzhin no// sgyu 'phrul thal
9a4(1): ba'i rgyud chen po las/ thabs chen lta ba'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// // de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba// thabs dang shes rab gnyis med pa'i// bde chen sku gsung thugs dkyil 'khor// 'di dag legs
9a5(1): par bshad par bya// 'gro drug ma bcos rang byung sku// lus gnas rtsa dang 'khor lor bcas// ma lus kun la khyab gnas pa// rang byung bde ba'i 'khor lo'i sku// rang byung rtsa yi 'khor lo na// so so'i yi ge
9a6(1): gang gnas pa// gsung gi dkyil 'khor kun dang 'brel// rang byung gsung gi 'khor lor bshad// gang du bcud kyi thig le yis// bde ba chen po'i ro ldan pas// ma skyes lhun grub rang gsal ba// khyab
9b1(1): pa thugs kyi 'khor lor bshad// thabs dang shes rab 'brel ba yi// gsang dbang pad+mar ldan gyur pa// thabs bzhi nyi zla 'dzag 'bar bas// sa yang bcu gsum bde gang ba// rang snang sku yi dkyil 'khor
9b2(1): nyid// steng 'og thabs kyi sbyor ba las// sprul pa'i thig le yang 'dug yi ge 'od thim pas// sgra dang bcas pa'i bde ba ni// rang snang gsung gi dkyil 'khor nyid// steng 'og dngas snyigs phye ba las// g.yas g.yon
9b3(1): gnyis med gsang ba'i lam// dgug dang bkug pa'i thabs nyid ni// byed pa sdom pa'i thabs kyis mtshon// rang byung ye shes lnga yi ro// khyab pa'i tshul gyis snang bar byed// nyi zla gsang sbyor thig le
9b4(1): las// gnas dang bstims nas dbyer med pas// ma lus bde chen lhan cig skyes// rang rig ma bcos mngon sum gsal// gnas dang 'byung ba ma lus pa// rang rig ye shes gzugs su skye// de nyid bde/
9b5(1): bar rang gsal ba// rang snang thugs kyi dkyil 'khor yin// rang byung thig le nyams skyes pa// dbab dang rten gyi phyag rgya las// bzung ba'i rlung la 'gro 'od med// bzlog pa thugs kyi sa bon can// 'di
9b6(1): ni thabs ldan gang zag la// 'khor ba'i bag chags ma lus pa// pad+ma rdo rje'i man ngag gis// nyi 'od mun pa bzhin du sel// bskyod pa thabs bzhis 'od zer gyis// thig le a la cung zad phog/ rang byung /
10a1(1): gsal ba'i lam du 'dri la// ha yi pad+mar 'byung ba la// thugs kyi sa bon zabs bcas pas// rang rang 'khor lor thim pa ni// chu la chu ltar gnas par byed// lan tshwa chu la thim pa ltar// ma lus
10a2(1): bde chen snying por thim// ma lus rang rig bde chen te// tha dad gnyis pa'i chos med de// sems med bde chen snying por gsal// skye med stong pa'i thig ler thim// 'gro ba ma lus thams cad dag/ gnas
10a3(1): pa'i stobs ni zad pa na// 'dus pa lnga yi rim pa yis// bag chags snying por rang zad nas// 'od gsal stong par snang bas na// re dogs med pa nam mkha' bzhin// bar mar sgyu ma'i lus thob nas// ma
10a4(1): 'ongs longs spyod rdzogs par bshad// nyi zla 'dres shing zung 'jug pas// sprul pa gzugs kyi skur 'gyur ro// gnas pa thabs kyis gsal byas pas// rang byung sku gsum lhun gyis grub// gsang sngags rdo
10a5(1): rje'i thabs chen gyis// 'khor ba'i rgyu 'bras zag pa rnams// gser 'gyur 'od dang bdud rtsi ltar// bde ba chen por byin gyis brlab// sku gsung thugs kyi thig le nyid// thabs dang shes rab las byung
10a6(1): nas// nyi zla yi ge'i stobs dag gis// brjod bral rang gi mtshan nyid mthong // a las byung ba'i gsang thig le// rang snang 'khor lor gnas brgyud pa// chu las byung ba'i thig le ltar// a las byung zhing a
10b1(1): la thim// rol pa sgyu 'phrul dra ba las// ma brjod gsung nyid rang snang bas// ma lus brjod bral bde ba'i gsung // skal ldan rnams la rang bzhin snang // nam mkha' rin chen phog pa ltar// thig le bde bas
10b2(1): rgyas btab nas// phyogs bcu dus bzhi'i sku gsung thugs// bde chen zag med rgyas par 'gyur// rang snang sku yi 'khor lo la// rang bzhin gsung gi dkyil 'khor nyid// g.yas dang g.yon gyis dbye ba
10b3(1): yis// sde tshan brgyad dang byed pa dang // khyab 'jug gsum yang de bzhin te// rim par bkod pas rang snang bas// 'jig rten 'das dang ma 'das pa'i// ji snyed bsgyur ba'i las rnams 'byung // rgyal ba bzhi
10b4(1): bcu rtsa lnga yi// ngo bo nyid du nges pas na// khu ba rtsa yi gzugs dag gis// sku gsung thugs dang ye shes lngar// ma btsal lhun gyis grub pa'o// rten gyi dkyil 'khor gang brten pa// sku dang gsung thugs yon
10b5(1): tan ni// rgyu dang lam dang 'bras bu dang // lus can khyab pa'i rang bzhin te// chu yi 'khor lo dbyibs kyi tshul// gang la thabs kyi rkyen gyur cing // bde ba bskyod dang smin pa las// dbyibs dang tshul ni dbang
10b6(1): drag yin// gyen du 'dren dang thur du bskul// 'khor lo bzhi la rgyas 'debs yin// gsang ba'i lam nas thabs bskul ba// brgyud pa'i lam ni sku gsung thugs// sum cu rtsa gnyis khyab pa'i rtsa// 'byung
11a1(1): ba'i thig le gnas pa'i sa// yi ge so so mdangs dang ldan// ngo bo nyid de ma bcos pa// bzhi gnyis 'dab ma'i snying po la// chos nyid ye shes yon tan rtsa// rang rgyud bzhi la yan lag
11a2(1): brgyad// 'od bzhi drangs snyigs sa bon drug/ snying po rang bzhin sku gsung thugs// gnyis med 'brel ba'i rang bzhin gnas// brgyad gnyis ldan pa'i ge sar la// AM gnas 'dab ma A li can// gsung gi
11a3(1): 'khor lo rten dang yul// pad+ma kha phye lta bu la// 'dus pa'i snying po sbyor ba'i tshul// lus can sgra rnams gsal bar 'byung // sprul pa drug cu bzhi gnas pa// sum cu rtsa gnyis rang bzhin ni// thig le 'phro 'du
11a4(1): gnas dang ldan// rdo rje'i pad+ma'i rtse dang 'brel// zin dang ma zin khyad par las// bde ba zag pa yod med 'byung // steng 'og thabs kyi rang bzhin la// 'phel dang sdud par shes par bya// lus can kun la pho
11a5(1): brang ste// thig le 'khyil ba lha nyid do// ro lngas kun la rgyas btab pas// sku gsung thugs su smin par byed// sgyu 'phrul rol pa thabs kyi rgyud// lhag pa'i thal rgyud chen po 'di// dbang dang skal med ske bo
11a6(1): la// 'chad cing ston pa ltung bar 'gyur// yab yum gsang ba'i thig le la// rang byung thabs kyi snying pos brtags// de ni kun gyi snying po ste// goms pas thams cad grub par 'gyur// gsang ba thabs chen
11b1(1): mngon snang ba// bdag nyid stobs ldan nus goms pas// phyi nang spyod yul bcas pa dag/ bde chen ngo bo nyid du nub// rang rgyud dag pa'i skye bo la// dbang bskur man ngag las goms na// longs spyod ldan
11b2(1): pa'i tshe 'di yis// bde ba chen po lhun grub 'gyur// lhag pa'i byang chub sems bde ba// ma lus snying por gsal thim pas// byed spyod ldan pa'i thabs chen gyis// rigs bdag rdo rje 'dzin pa 'grub// bde
11b3(1): bas bde ba gang goms na// bdag nyid chen po bde ba la// dngas snyigs med cing 'phel 'grib med// rgya mtsho'i chu lhar ro gcig pas// bde ba chen po gcig tu gnas// sgyu 'phrul thal ba'i rgyud chen po
11b4(1): las// rang byung sku gsung thugs kyi le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba// thabs dang shes rab rol pa las// bde ba chen po rang snang ba'i// sgrub pa'i cho ga bshad par bya// dman dang
11b5(1): bde ba med pa la// mtshan ma'i spros pa zhen pa yis// bde chen nyams la mi gnas pas// thun mong dman pa 'byung 'gyur gyi// mchog la reg zad reg pa med// 'di ni zab mo gsang ba ste// gsang ba las
11b6(1): kyang 'byung 'gyur zhing // mchog gi snying po sbas pa'i don// gsang ba'i gter ni rab 'byin pa// 'gro ba chags pa can don du// dug gis dug nad sel ba ltar// thabs mchog dbang las byung ba yi// dngos
12a1(1): grub bzang po mchog 'byung ba'o// gang du yo byad mchog gyur pa// rtsa ba gnyis las lngar gyur pa// mchog tu gyur pa kun 'grub cing // gal te nyams na 'jig par 'gyur// rang byung bde
12a2(1): ba'i thig le ni// gsang ba bcud las 'byung ba ste// zag pa med pa'i thig le la// re dogs mtshan ma'i yul las 'das// kha dog gnas dbyibs 'dzin med pas// bde chen chos dbyings rtog dpyod
12a3(1): bral// thabs dang shes rab yongs rdzogs pa'i// phyi nang snod bcud ma lus pa// dngos dang dngos med dbyer med par// rtog pa thabs kyis dbang bsgyur ba// dbyer med bde ba lhun gyis grub// rten dang
12a4(1): brten pa dbyer med pa'i// bde ba'i thig le de bzhin nyid// 'du 'phro 'byung bzhi de bzhin nyid// bde chen sems kyi rtsa bar bshad// rang byung bde ba chen po ni// rtogs las goms pa gsal ba las// bde
12a5(1): chen bsam yas 'bras bu 'byung // ngo bo min la rang snang ba// lus dang rtsa dang bcud rnams la// thig le bye brag bsam yas 'phro// bde bas 'jig bral nyams pa med// rang byung rol pa'i bde ba yang // sku
12a6(1): ma bde ba'i mchog tu gsungs// thabs dang shes rab gnyis med pa'i// rol pa sngags te phyag rgya'i gar// thabs dang ldan pas brten goms pas// dngos grub ji ltar 'dod pa 'byung // thabs dang shes pa
12b1(1): byin rlabs pas// phyag rgya chen por bstan pa yis// b+ha ga'i rgyan dang nam mkha'i khams// rdo rje thig le mnyam sbyar bas// gsang ba'i mkha' lnga 'byung bar 'gyur// de las ye shes skye bar 'gyur// sra ba dang
12b2(1): ni gsher dang drod// go 'byed bskyod pa'i rang bzhin la// nyi ma zla ba 'dzag pa las// lhan cig skyes pa'i bde ba 'byung // bcud dang bde la goms 'gyur zhing // gar thabs rlung la dbang bskur bas// rtsa ba
12b3(1): yan lag nad 'tsho zhing // bde chen bdud rtsis ring du 'tsho// lus dang rtsa dang sems kyi snod// gsang ba longs spyod lnga yis tshims// mun pa la ni snang ba bzhin// dngos po bde ba chen por 'gyur// thog ma
12b4(1): med par las bsags pas// rtog pa'i bag chags sel ba yis// thams cad skye mched dbyings su gsal// gang du thabs kyis zin pas na// gzugs dang nyi zla'i thig ler bcas// thabs dang bskyod pa'i
12b5(1): rang bzhin gyis// rten ni gnas su dgug pa dang // de btang ba ni skabs kyis te// dgang dang dgang bas bcing bya zhing // rten dang thig ler rig par bcas// thabs kyis leg par dgrol bar bya// lus
12b6(1): bcud nyams dang thig ler bcas// thabs kyi cho gas gso byas na// las dang nyon mongs sdug bsngal ba// bsad pas 'pham rten rgyal bar 'gyur// dngos grub kun 'byung snying po'i thabs// rang byung rgyal po
13a1(1): gsal bya'i phyir// thabs chen gsang ba'i man ngag gis// gser 'gyur sman dang mun sel bzhin// bcud kyi bdag nyid rgyas pa yis// gnyis med gsal bar ldan pa ni// bzang dang bdud
13a2(1): rtsir ldan pa des// bde chen ngo bo mi 'gyur ba// dpal ldan skyob pa'i phyag rgya yis// ma lus thebs par gnas pa yin// gang nus med dang dka' thub dang // dbang dang mi ldan sgro skur dang // thabs bral

13a4(1): kyang // thabs dang bral bas mthong ba med// rang byung rten can dkyil 'khor drug/ gsang ba'i thabs kyis gnas pa yin// bcud 'dus thig le chen po ni// bde chen kun gyi snying po ste// thabs kyi nyams su
13a5(1): ngas pa las// 'bras bu yid bzhin nor bu bzhin// 'di nyid sgyu 'phrul dra ba ste// dkyil 'khor kun gyi ngo bo yin// gnas pa sgrol ma rlung gis bskyod// 'bar ba de steng rkyen gyis te// chu khams 'khor lo
13a6(1): rim zhu bas// mi tshugs ye shes nam mkha'i gzugs// thabs dang bcas pas rten thig le// sgrol ma rlung la goms pa yis// gsang ba'i las la thogs pa med// lus la sdug bsngal mi 'byung zhing // phyi nang

13b2(1): longs spyod rdzogs par 'gyur// drag da la 'jam pa'i mtshan nyid ni// snyigs ma zad pa'i thabs yin te// phyi nang rgyu ba'i khyad par gyis// 'pho ba bcu drug shes par bya// snyigs ma dwangs mar ma zhugs
13b3(1): na// nad dang sdug bsngal gdung ba dang // bde chen nyid la bar chad 'byung // snyigs ma drangs ma la 'jug pa// rtags ni sna tshogs 'byung bar 'gyur// brtan na bar chad med par skye// gsal na dngos po bde/

14a1(1): pa la// bde ba 'phel 'grib mi 'byung bas// thams cad bde chen dkyil 'khor mchog/ nam mkha'i mtha' bzhin khyab par gsal// gang du 'phel ba gsal byed pa// ma thob pa dang rgyun bcas

14b2(1): ba'i thig le chen po nyid// rtsa dang thig le'i tshul dag gis// thams cad khyab pa'i tshul gyis gnas// gnyis su med pa bde ba'i rgyu// nyi zla khu bar gnas pa yi// sems lnga skyed pa 'brel ba yi// bde ba'i ro/

24a4(1): ba'i sa bon te// bskal pa bye bar srin bur ltung // ma chags thabs bral 'khor ba ste// chags pa thabs bral 'khor ba nyid// thabs chen ldan pa'i rnal 'byor la// thams cad bde ba chen por gnas// thig
24a5(1): le chen po'i rang bzhin la// ji ltar yon tan kun 'dus pas// thabs zin ros ni nam mkha' ltar// thams cad khyab pa'i tshul du snang // rang byung bde ba'i thig le nyid// zin nas gsang ba'i mthar phyin
24a6(1): pas// dang po rten can dbang po lnga// bde ba'i thig les rgyas btab la// de nas rten med nyams myong gis// thabs dang 'dzin pa bsam yas pas// thams cad bde chen ngo bor gsal// ji snyed chos kun ma
24b1(1): lus pa// rgya mtsho la ni chu klung ltar// tha dad snang ba ma yin te// bde chen thig le'i ngo bor thim// rang byung nyams la brtan thos pas// phyi nang bde chen rang rig pas// shes pa 'jug pa'i yul las
24b2(1): 'das// rig pa'i thig le skye ba med// bde chen thig le khyab pa la// rlung dang thig le 'gro 'od med// 'phel ba med cing 'grib pa med// rgyu 'bras med cing rim pa med// nam mkha' la ni rang snang
24b3(1): bzhin// rtog pa'i dbang po dag pa las// dbang yul la sogs gang snang ba// bde ba chen po'i rang bzhin gsal// 'dis ni nam mkha'i mthar thug par// chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam par// bde ba
24b4(1): chen po chos kyi dbyings// gsang ba gnyis med dag pa'o// sangs rgyas kun gyi bsngags pa yi// gsang ba'i dam tshig chen po 'di// mu stegs can dang dka' thub can// dman pa'i rigs can yul ma
24b5(1): yin// bde ba med pa'i chags bral 'di// nam mkha' la ni myu gu ltar// bde ba chen po thig le nyid// 'byung bar nus pa ma yin no// thig le thabs kyis ma zin pa// gang gis zhen pas de spyad pas// tha mal
24b6(1): pa dang mu stegs kyi// log pa'i lam du ltung 'gyur bas// zag pas rgas dang rgud pa dang // nyams dang brgyal dang nad gzir dang // log pa'i gdung bas gzir ba dang // rigs ngan mngal du skye bar
25a1(1): 'gyur// rtag tu 'dod la zhen pa ni// de bzhin zhen pas sel bar byed// spong dang 'geg pa sred 'phel te// dbul po yo byad bral ba bzhin// bde chen thig le'i man ngag 'di// rig pa so sor
25a2(1): gnas su bstim// bskyod pa ha yis bskul ba yis// bdag nyid chen po lnga yi rgyun// steng sgo nas byung bde ba'i bcud// so so'i bzhi bcu gnyis la thim// kun nas bde ba'i ye shes che// rgyal ba mnyes pa'i
25a3(1): mchog tu gsungs// bco brgyad phrag gnyis bum pa dang // drug gnyis gzer gyis sbyangs nas ni// dbang bskur byin rlabs bde thob pa// theg pa chen por dbugs phyung ba'o// dbul ba'i khyad par dang
25a4(1): sbyar nas// dkyil 'khor gnyis la brten goms nas// phra ba'i khyad par nas bsam nas// nam mkha'i mthar zug bar du bya// phyi nang gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor du// bya ba'i las rnams mthar phyin
25a5(1): nas// 'jug dang nyams rnyed bla ma yis// slob ma'i rim pa smin pa'i phyir// 'jug pa'i cho ga tshul bzhin bya// dkyil 'khor gang dang 'tshams pa la/ 'jug pa'i cho ga rgyas byas pas// bdag gzhan nus pa
25a6(1): mthar phyin pas// bde chen lhun gyis grub par 'gyur// bla med dbang phyug mnyes bya'i phyir// rigs sam yang na 'byor pa yi// ser sna spangs pa'i zang zing dag/ phongs pa med pa'i sems kyis dbul// gang
25b1(1): du dad dang brtson 'grus dang // brtul zhugs gsum dang ldan pa la// sa bon 'jug dang nus byed nas// bde ba'i dbang ni rim bzhin sbyin// phyag rgya chen po nam mkha'i dbyings// sor bzhi tshad du rang
25b2(1): bzhin gnas// bde ba ye shes thugs dkyil 'khor// kha dog dbyibs dang ldan par bya// thabs kyi rang gnas cho gar ldan// 'jug pa pos kyang gsol ba gdab// thabs dang shes rab nyi zla'i 'bru// phra mo
25b3(1): gsal ba'i rang bzhin la// rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor lhun rdzogs pa// gsal bar gnas pa bris pa yin// thal mo zhes bya sdebs pa'i sgra// dbang po yul du rab sbyor bas// phyag rgya chen po nam mkha'i
25b4(1): dbyings// brtul zhugs chen po'i dang du blangs// rdo rje mdzub mo'i rtse dag tu// til 'bru nam mkha'i gzhal yas su// ri rab gcig gi phyag rgya dgod// thabs kyi cho ga rab gnas bya// gsang ba'i cho ga
25b5(1): lugs su dbul// dbang bsgyur phyag rgya la gnas pas// rang byung thig le rgya tshigs 'grub// bcu drug tshul gyis 'grub pa ni// gsang ba'i yo byad ldan pa yi// gsang ba'i gnas la sbyar brtson pas// zla ba
25b6(1): 'phel ba'i rim pa bzhin// bde ba chen po rdzogs par 'gyur// ma nyams thabs dang nyams ldan pas// lo zla tshes grangs rab 'bring gis// dbang bsgyur phyag rgya la gnas pas// rang byung thig le sna tshogs
26a1(1): 'grub// bcu drug tshul gyis 'grub pa ni// bdag gzhan bya ba mthar phyin pa// bde chen stong nyid thig le la// rol pa'i thig ler rang shar ba// dgag bsgrub med pa'i tshul gyis snang // bde
26a2(1): 'dus ye shes thig le la// mtha' yas ye shes rang snang ba// rang byung thig le bde chen las// ma btsal lhun grub rig 'dzin mchog/ bde chen rig pa las byung ba'i// zhing khams gzhal yas sku
26a3(1): gsung thugs// gcig dang du ma las 'das pa// gsang ba chen po'i mtshan nyid do// de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba// thun mong byin rlabs dkyil 'khor du// rigs ldan brtson 'grus can dag la// rgyal po
26a4(1): lta bu gang byin pa// khams bcud bde ba'i lam nyid du// dbu ma bcud ldan mtshan ldan pa// dra ba'i rtsa dang dbang po dang // phung sogs ye shes bde 'khor lo// hUM gi bde ba ye shes bcas// tshogs brgyad rang
26a5(1): bzhin ye shes lnga// sngags rdzas dgongs pas gang bslangs pa// kun nas ldan zhing skyob pa yis// sdug bsngal las grol rigs su nges// spyi mgrin snying dang yan lag sogs// rang byung rten gyi thig le
26a6(1): las// rigs kyi phyag rgya gsal ldan pa// gnyis med thim pa'i byin rlabs kyis// nus pa lnga ldan phyag rgyar smin// thabs kyi cho ga dbang bskur bas// rgyal mchog rgyas btab phyag rgya'i mchog/ rgyal mchog
26b1(1): nyid du grub pa yin// thabs dang shes rab byin rlabs kyis// mi spyod yab yum rol pa las// bde ba gsal zhing dmigs pa la// shes rab thabs kyi phyag rgya'o// rdo rje ye shes hUM tshogs kyis// pad+ma ye shes
26b2(1): bsdus 'khyil ba'i// nyung dkar tshad tsam rdo rje sems// rtse nas rtse ru phyin pa yis// rang bzhin chos khams dkyil 'khor gyis// sa bon zung gsum gnyid dang bcas// gnas ngan len pa gsum sbyangs
26b3(1): te// dmigs med sems kyi ye shes lnga// gsal bas sa bon tshig pa bzhin// mi skye thabs kyis dbugs phyung ba'o// de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba// rjes su 'jug pa'i phyag rgya nyid// zil ba'i thig le sngon
26b4(1): lam bzhin// bcu drug phyed phyed thig le gcig/ phan tshun bkod pa'i sdom gyis bsdam// bde ba gnyis pa'i ngo bo nyid// gsum pa ye shes dkyil 'khor du// gsal ba'i bshad pa gyur pa'i sgra// rang bzhin
26b5(1): 'od gsal dkyil 'khor ro// de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba// rdo rje nyi ma thabs kyi rgya// phung sogs phyag rgya'i tshogs dang ldan// de zla bsil byed shes rab dngos// dus gcig ro mnyam thig le che// sum cu
26b6(1): rtsa gnyis mtshan rdzogs shing // zla ba ye shes lnga bcu drug/ dpe byad la sogs dpag tu med// sems shes mngon par shes dang ldan// sems mtha' 'gro yi rdzu 'phrul che// gnas nas log par thim pa'i
27a1(1): sgras// mtha' gnyis ma gos pad+ma can// sprul pa'i gnas nas skye ba yis// bzhi bcu rtsa lnga rdzogs mtha' yas// kun dang gzhan nyid rang gsal bas// bcu gsum yi ge 'khor lo brjod// rgyal
27a2(1): ba kun gyi sku gsung thugs// dbyer med thig le ngo bo nyid// dbang bskur lnga yi khyad par te// skal ldan rnams la bstan pa yin// gong du bskal pa bye ba yi// thun mong thun mong ma yin pa'i// sdig pa byas pa
27a3(1): gang yin dang // dka' thub sdom pas lus gdungs shing // sdug bsngal nye bar gzir ba kun// dbang bskur thabs kyis tshe 'dir grol// sgyu 'phrul thal ba'i rgyud chen po las/ dbang bskur bar bshad pa'i

27b3(1): pa'i brtul zhugs pa'o// spang len can dang dgag bsgrub can// gnyen po can dang dka' thub can// khrus dang gtsang sgra gang spyad pa// mnyam nyid bde chen rtul zhugs spyod pa 'di// theg dman log rtog
27b4(1): spangs pa yi// byang chub rdo rje can sogs pa'i// bde chen sras dang bcas pa'i don// lta spyod gol zhing log pa ni// rtsi sman rang gi srog gcod ltar// thabs bral spyod pas grol 'dod pa'i// rnal 'byor bdud

54a5(1): 'phel 'grib mi gnas dang // thabs chen skal ldan spyod yul de// gzhan la mi gnas spyod yul min// bskal pa bye bar mi 'byang ba'i// las dang nyon mongs sdug bsngal dang // sgrib pa bag chags thams
54a6(1): cad kun// thabs chen gsang bas mngon du sel// dka' thub gdung bas lus gzir cing // lus sems sdug bsngal dbang bsgyur ba'i// sangs rgyas sras su gyur pas kyang // phyogs tsam reg par nus ma
54b1(1): yin// kun gyis spangs pa'i chags sdang lnga// 'dod lnga dran rtog phra rags bcas// thabs kyis de dag zil mnan nas// rnal 'byor bde ba'i pha rol phyin// tshad ma gzhan dang bral ba yi// rang rig bde chen
54b2(1): byang chub sems// ngo bo rtog dpyod las 'das pa// 'gro 'ong mi yul bsam las 'das// thams cad byang chub snying po mchog/ gang phyir bde ba ye shes ni// cho ga thabs las shes par 'gyur// thabs
54b3(1): bral thabs las rnam par 'jog/ rang bzhin thabs kyi pha rol phyin// thabs chen bde bas gang rtogs pa// bde bas dka' thub zil gyis gnon// sgyu 'phrul dra ba mngon rdzogs pa// thabs chen gsang
54b4(1): ba'i thig le ni// rtogs shing goms par grol 'gyur te// gzhan gyis nam yang 'grub ma yin// rang bzhin rtogs goms byin rlabs kyis// dper na nyi 'od rin chen bzhin// las dang bsod nams rkyen dag
54b5(1): las// chu dang me long gzugs brnyan ltar// dngos po ji ltar gsal ba ltar// thabs dang man ngag stobs kyis 'grub// sgyu 'phrul chen po thig le nyid// thabs dang shes rab gsal 'gyur bas// bde ba
54b6(1): gsal la mi rtog pa// thams cad mkhyen pa'i stobs su snang // rang nyid phyag rgya stobs chen gyis// mi mthun gnyen po bral ba las// thabs chen gsang ba mthar phyin pas// man ngag ldan pas 'grub 'gyur
55a1(1): te// rang rig yon tan mngon snang bzhin// bye brag brgyad cu la sogs pa// bstan pa'i khyad par ci snyed pa// 'dul ba'i dbang gis snang ba ste// gsang ba 'dis ni rtogs par 'gyur// gang med
55a2(1): de nyid mi 'byung phyir// dper na lus dang yan lag bzhin// dus gsum sangs rgyas bstan par bcas// rang byung bstan pa rgya mtshor 'dus// bskal pa bye ba bsam yas par// thabs dang dka' bas gang
55a3(1): btsal bas// zab mo'i thabs rgyud mi mthong ste// zab mo rgyal ba'i dgongs par bshad// phyi nang gsang ba la sogs pa// thabs chen bstan pa gang gsungs pa// thams cad yan lag snang ba ste// kun gyi snying
55a4(1): po 'di gsungs pa'o// zhing khams phyi nang bsam yas par// gleng gzhi gleng bslang rtog pa dang // cho ga'i dkyil 'khor grangs med par// thams cad 'dir gnas pa nyid do// 'das dang ma byon da ltar
55a5(1): ba'o// sangs rgyas rnal 'byor thams cad kyi// lam mchog gsang ba 'di yin te// 'byung gnas 'byung nyid de phyir ro// khyad par thabs chen sgyu 'phrul 'di// gsang ba'i gsang mchog dam pa 'di// gzhan dang
55a6(1): dbang po dman pa dang // ma dag pa la ma gnang ngo // rnal 'byor gsang bar zhugs rnams kyis// gsang chen rol pa'i thal rgyud las// dbang dang man ngag stobs kyis brtag/ tshe 'di nyid la 'grub par
55b1(1): 'gyur// dka' thub gdung ba kun bral zhing // longs spyod lnga ldan cho ga yis// 'dus pa med pa'i spyod pa yis// 'jigs pa med par rnam par grol// nam mkha' lta bur gang rtogs pas// rgyal po'i spyod pa
55b2(1): la brten na// bar chad med par gsal goms pas// yid bzhin nor bu lta bur 'gyur// gzhan yang gsang chen thig le ni// gsang ba'i yid 'phrog thabs kyi rgyud// ma lus thabs kyis rol spyad na// skad
55b3(1): cig tsam gyis grol bar 'gyur// ma lus 'ching ba yul gyi dug/ rgyal ba'i dgongs pas dbang bsgyur nas// phyi nang yul sems snod bcud bcas// thabs chen bde bar mngon du gsal// bye ba brgya phrag mang
55b4(1): po'i tshogs// lha rnams dang ni klu rnams dang // 'gro ba skal ldan thams cad kyis// 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga rnams la// ci 'dod par ni spyod bzhin du// dag pa dang ni bde ba dang // yid bde ba dang sems
55b5(1): bde bas// ma lus gsang ba nyid du blta// rnal 'byor pho mor 'brel ba yis// ma lus tshogs la longs spyod cing // blta dang bgad dang 'khyud pa dang // dbang po thug dang zhal la sogs// phrad dang spyad pa
55b6(1): la sogs pas// dga' zhing nyams dang thig le bzhi// lus sems dga' bar grol bar 'gyur// byin rlabs thabs kyi nyams ldan pas// nyams dang re dogs med pa yis// glu dang gar dang rol
56a1(1): pa'i thabs// sna tshogs thabs ni ston par mdzad// ma dag pa dang mi 'tshams shing // dag pa la 'tshams re dogs med// thabs spyod bye brag mtha' yas pa// ma bcos thabs kyi spyod par
56a2(1): gnas// gsang chen rnal 'byor spyod pa 'di// dga' dang sbyangs pa'i rang bzhin las// gzhan dang byis pa tha mal dang // sgro skur ya gar gnas la sogs// byin na bar chad 'byung 'gyur te// dmyal ba yi/
56a3(1): dwags byol song sogs// bskal pa rdul snyed gnas 'gyur te// bde bas phongs pa nyid du 'gyur// bskal pa zhing gi rdul snyed du// sbyangs dang bsags pa gang yin pa// skal ldan 'ga' yi spyod yul
56a4(1): te// bsgrub bya'i 'bras bu snying po nyid// gsang ba chen po thal ba'i rgyud// ma lus dag pa'i 'jig rten du// skad cig byin rlabs snang mdzad pa// gsang chen rmad byung theg par bshad// sgyu 'phrul thal ba'i rgyud
56a5(1): chen po las/ gsang ba theg chen bstan pa'i le'u ste nyi shu gnyis pa'o// // de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba// rtog pa kun las rab 'das pa// brtag pa kun gyi ngo bo nyid// sgyu 'phrul dra bas mngon snang
56a6(1): ba// sangs rgyas kun gyi rang bzhin ni// dag dang ma dag khyad par gyis// phyi nang yul sems dbang por bcas// ma bcos rang rig dbyings su 'dus// 'khor dang mya ngan 'das pa yang // gzhi rtsa med
56b1(1): dbyings skad cig ma// mi gnas tshul gyis gnas 'gyur te// de la gnas pa gang yang med// 'byung ba lnga dang phung po lnga// khams dang skye mched la sogs pa// thabs dang shes rab ldan gyur pa'i// gnyis su
56b2(1): med par rang bzhin gnas// rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor rdul snyed pa// zhing dang longs spyod mdzad pa dang // ma lus gnyis med snang ba ste// dbyer med rig pa rang snang ngo // phyi dang nang dang yul sems
56b3(1): dang // ji snyed spyod yul 'gyur ba kun// nam mkha' la ni gza' skar ltar// chos kyi dbyings las don 'byung ste// bya byed med par ngang gis snang // phyi nang gsang bar bcas pa yi// kun gzhi thabs kyis
56b4(1): gsal byas pas// ma lus rang snang 'jig rten pas// spang dang spang bar bya ba med// dbang po yul dus rnam shes tshogs// ma lus gnyis med rang snang ba// skyes bu thabs kyi spyod yul te// skal ldan dag
56b5(1): gis shes par bya// thugs kyi bde ba chos kyi dbyings// rang rig bsam pa'i yul las 'das// de nyid ji ltar gsal ba ltar// thabs kyi rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs 'dzin// gang dag gang la dbang ba ni// 'di ni
56b6(1): dbang po mchog tu gsungs// brten pa'i shes rab bcas pa yi// dmigs par bya ba'i yul nyid do// ji snyed chos rnams bsam yas pa// thun mong thun mong ma yin pa'i// rten gyi bya ba thams cad
57a1(1): kyang // dbang po yul du 'dus par bshad// ji snyed chos rnams rdul snyed pa// 'jig rten 'jig rten 'das pa yis// nang dang phyi ru bstan pa kun// rang rig ye shes mchog tu gsungs// thabs
57a2(1): mkhas bye brag cir bstan pa// thabs kyi khyad par snang ba yin// e ma gar mkhan 'khor lo bde// ma skyes stong pa'i rang bzhin las// sgyu 'phrul dra ba bde ba'i mchog/ gsang dbang pad+mar 'brel ba na// bde

57a5(1): las// ji snyed chos kun rang bzhin 'char// thams cad thig le bde chen la// yul dbang phyi nang spro bsdu med// rang byung thabs kyi sgyu 'phrul ni// dkyil 'khor kun gyi thabs bcud de// thabs dang shes rab
57a6(1): 'brel pa las// 'bras bu rang bzhin gsal bar 'char// thabs la stong pas rgyas btab cing // stong pa la ni bde bas btab// ro gcig bde ba chen po rgyas// phyi nang yul sems kun tu btab// ma lus
57b1(1): bde chen thig le ste// dngos po nam yang yod ma yin// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas par// gnyis med bde ba rol pa'i mchog/ gsang ba dbang gi cho ga las// bde chen lam la bar chad med// dbang
57b2(1): po mchog gi yul du gyur// de bas gzhan gyi spyod yul min// sangs rgyas kun gyis byin brlabs pa'i// rang rig bde chen gnyis med 'di// man ngag thabs kyis mtshon pa las// tshig dang yi ge'i spyod yul

58a1(1): por thim// brtags pa'i bye brag sna tshogs pa// ngo bo nyid ni cir snang yang // rang bzhin ngang la dbyer med de// thams cad ma bcos ngang du zhi// ma byas rang byung rang snang bas// yul dang dbang

97a3(1): 'grub 'gyur// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal sbyor bas/ mthu nyid kyis ni thamams cad du// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' yas pa'i// bud med mchog rnams skye bar 'gyur// de yi dam tshig de byung ba// sdug pa'i

97b4(1): mchod// rnal 'byor thams cad bde ba yi// rjes su sbyor bas mchod byed cing // rtag tu myong bar byed pa na// shin tu sbyor bas rab 'grub 'gyur// sangs rgyas thams cad bdag nyid kyi// ra sa ya na bde ba
